    if (_WF.utils.isManagedPrivacyGeo()) {
        /* Cross browser event handler definition */
        var eventMethod = window.addEventListener ? 'addEventListener' : 'attachEvent';
        var messageEvent = eventMethod === 'attachEvent' ? 'onmessage' : 'message';
        var eventer = window[eventMethod];
        var subs = {};
        /* Callback to be executed when any event is fired */
        function receiveMessage(event) {
            function eventDataContains(str) {
                return JSON.stringify(event.data).indexOf(str) !== -1;
            }
            if (event && event.data) {
                Object.keys(subs)
                    .filter(function(key) {
                        return eventDataContains(key)
                    })
                    .forEach(function(key) {
                        subs[key] = subs[key].filter(function(obj) {
                            setTimeout(function() {
                                obj.action(event.data);
                            }, 0);
                            if (obj.once) {
                                return false;
                            }
                            return true;
                        });
                    });
            }
        }
        /* Register event handler */
        eventer(messageEvent, receiveMessage, false);
        /* Callback to be fired when message is received */
        function subscribe(eventName, action, once) {
            subs[eventName] = subs[eventName] || [];
            subs[eventName].push({
                action: action,
                once: once
            });
        }

        function remove(el) {
            if (el.parentNode) {
                el.parentNode.removeChild(el);
            }
        }

        function find(selector) {
            return Array.prototype.slice.call(document.querySelectorAll(selector));
        }

        function flatten(out, arr) {
            return out.concat(arr);
        }

        function collectElements(selectorList) {
            return selectorList
                .map(find)
                .reduce(flatten, []);
        }

        function synchronizeClicks(el, idx, switches) {
            switches.forEach(function(elm) {
                elm.click();
            });
            el && el[eventMethod]('mouseup', function() {
                setTimeout(function() {
                    switches
                        .filter(function(elm) {
                            return elm !== el
                        })
                        .map(function(elm) {
                            elm.click();
                            return elm;
                        })
                }, 0);
                message('slider_click');
            }, false);
            return el;
        }

  
00006000
      function getConsentState(fn) {
            __cmp('getVendorConsents', null, function(result) {
                var purposeConsents = result.purposeConsents;
                var consentState = Object.keys(purposeConsents)
                    .reduce(function(out, key) {
                        return purposeConsents[key] && out;
                    }, true);
                fn(consentState);
            });
        }

        function clearCCPALink() {
            var link = document.querySelector(".ccpa-click");
            if (link) {
                link.parentElement.removeChild(link);
            }
        }

        function message(action) {
            var cg = function(key) {
                return _WF.cache.getItem(key);
            };
            var sendMessage = function(consentState) {
                var bi = _WF.utils.getBrowserInfo();
                var msg = [
                    'hive_cmp_action',
                    action,
                    consentState,
                    cg(_WF.KEYS.SUBID) || '',
                    cg(_WF.KEYS.DEVICETYPE) || '',
                    cg(_WF.KEYS.BUCKETID) || '',
                    cg(_WF.KEYS.SESSIONTOKEN) || '',
                    cg(_WF.KEYS.POSTID),
                    cg(_WF.KEYS.PAGENUMBER),
                    cg(_WF.KEYS.SESSIONDEPTH) || '',
                    cg(_WF.KEYS.UUID) || '',
                    bi[_WF.BROWSERINFO.NAME],
                    bi[_WF.BROWSERINFO.VERSION]
                ];
                _WF.utils.track(msg);
            };
            getConsentState(sendMessage);
        }

        subscribe('oil_click_advanced_settings', function(ev) {
            function reveal() {
                var oil = document.getElementById('as-oil-cpc');
                oil.style.visibility = 'visible';
            }

            function format() {
                var elementsToRemove = ['.as-js-btn-deactivate-all', '.as-js-btn-activate-all', '.as-oil-cpc__status', '.as-js-oilback__icon'];
                collectElements(elementsToRemove)
                    .filter(function(el) {
                        return el;
                    })
                    .map(remove);
                var switches = ['.as-oil-cpc__slider'];
                collectElements(switches)
                    .map(synchronizeClicks);
                message('show_info');
            }

            function hide() {
                var oil = document.getElementById('as-oil-cpc');
                oil.style.visibility = 'hidden'
            }

            function init() {
                var oil = document.getElementById('as-oil-cpc');
                if (oil) {
                    hide();
                    format()
                    reveal();
                } else {
                    setTimeout(init, 5);
                }
            }
            init();
        });

        subscribe('oil_click_back_to_main', function(ev) {
            message('hide_info');
        });

        subscribe('oil_optin_done', function(ev) {
            clearCCPALink();
            getConsentState(function(consentState) {
                if (_WF.utils.isGDPRCountry()) {
                    _WF.cache.json.set(_WF.KEYS.COOKIECONSENT, consentState);
                }
                message('done');
            });
            var cmpResult = {};
            __cmp('getConsentData', null, function(result) {
                cmpResult.getConsentData = result;
                if (_WF.utils.isGDPRCountry()) {
                    _WF.cache.json.set(_WF.KEYS.CMPRESULT, cmpResult);
                }
            });
            __cmp('getVendorConsents', null, function(result) {
                cmpResult.getVendorConsents = result;
                if (_WF.utils.isGDPRCountry()) {
                    _WF.cache.json.set(_WF.KEYS.CMPRESULT, cmpResult);
                }
                if (_WF.utils.isCCPARegion() && result && result.purposeConsents) {
                    _WF.cache.json.set(_WF.KEYS.CMPCCPARESULT, {
                        state: 1,
                        value: result.purposeConsents["5"] === false ? "1YYY" : "1YNY"
                    });
                }
            });
        });

        subscribe('oil_click_thirdparty_list', function(ev) {
            message('3p_click');
        });

        subscribe('oil_click_company_list', function(ev) {
            message('company_click');
        });

        subscribe('oil_shown', function(ev) {
            message('render');
        });
